  • JsonConverter

Welcome to VHARM

VHARM is a security model designed to analyse cybersecurity in autonomous vehicles.

JSON Structure of in-vehicle network

The JSON structure of an in-vehicle network is illustrated below. This JSON data is then transformed into a structure suitable for visualising the VHARM

We have prepared the data in the next section that can be paste into IVHARM Visualization and Analysis which can automatically generate attack path and calculate security metrics

Baseline Scenario of BMW vehicle

Scenario Data using for the analysis

The scenario data used to generate the comparative analysis and security evaluation in Section 6 of the paper can be found below.

This JSON data has been prepared for use within the IVHARM Visualization and Analysis. Simply copy the JSON data into the input field. The results will display on the page, while other calculation metrics can be viewed in the console box (F12).

Baseline for BMW car

1. Baseline Scenario

Baseline for Tesla car

1. Baseline Scenario
